class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:albanian.html>Albanian</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">shtëng</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:harden.html>hardened</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:press.html>pressed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:matter.html>matter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit"><a href = vnd.unilang:sanskrit.html>Sanskrit</a></a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्त्यायते</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span </p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb"><a href = vnd.unilang:adverb.html>Adverb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stone.html>stone</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:comparable.html>comparable</a></i>)

annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stḗlē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:medical.html>medical</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:use.html>use</a> derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> 4 (<a href = vnd.unilang:seat.html>seat</a> used <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:defecation.html>defecation</a>).

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:strange.html>strange</a></strong> (<i>third-person <a href = vnd.unilang:singular.html>singular</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">stranges</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">stranging</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">stranged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:obsolete.html>obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:transitive.html>transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alienate.html>alienate</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:estrange.html>estrange</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:obsolete.html>obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:intransitive.html>intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> estranged <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> alienated.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:obsolete.html>obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:intransitive.html>intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wonder.html>wonder</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> astonished (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:something.html>something</a>).
